While the studio is often known for magical adventures like My Neighbor Totoro, this film is a devastatingly realistic war drama directed by Isao Takahata. ↵ Set in Kobe, Japan, during the final months of World War II, the story follows two siblings: Seita, a teenager, and his younger sister, Setsuko. After their mother is killed in an American firebombing raid and their father is missing in action serving in the Imperial Navy, the children are left to fend for themselves. ↵ Interestingly, director Isao Takahata often resisted the "anti-war" label. He intended the film to be a social critique of the isolation and pride of youth. He wanted to show how Seita’s decision to cut themselves off from society (by leaving their aunt's home to live alone) ultimately led to their tragedy. He felt that by isolating themselves, they lost the community support necessary for survival in such a brutal era. Id X

Easy for his systems to hit 99% accuracy when symptoms are neatly catecategorized in a spreadsheet.
